  <script>

let checkAdobeTargetInterval;

let checkElementInterval;



function triggerAtNotiClickEvent() {

    let element = document.querySelector('div.promotion button.cmp-button[aria-controls="promotion"]');

    if (element) {

        // 개인화 link click 버튼에 promotion button 클릭하는 함수 추가    

        var notificationBar = document.querySelectorAll("[personalized-message*='y'] .c-notification-banner__link");

        notificationBar.forEach(link => {

            link.setAttribute('href','javascript:void(0)')

            link.addEventListener('click', function(){document.querySelector('button[href="#Promotions"]').click();})

        })

      

        clearInterval(checkElementInterval); // Element를 찾았으므로 interval 체크를 중지

    }

}



function setAdobeTargetEventHandler() {

  document.addEventListener(adobe.target.event.REQUEST_SUCCEEDED, function(e) {  

      var tokens = e.detail.responseTokens;

      window.at_evt_all = e;

      window.at_res_all = e.detail;

      window.at_res_tokens = tokens;



      if (isEmpty(tokens)) { 

        return; 

      } 



      var uniqueTokens = distinct(tokens); 

      uniqueTokens.forEach(function(token) {      

        if(token["activity.name"] == "UK_GL_ALL_XT_ALL_NOTIFICATIONBAR_2308"){

          

          // if response comes from AEM, check rendering & fire impression call

          var observe_target = document.querySelector(".component>.cmp-container");

          var observerCallback = function(mutationList, observer){

            for(var mutation of mutationList){

              if(mutation.type == 'childList'){

                var addedNodes = [...mutation.addedNodes];

                var hasPersonalizedMessage = addedNodes.some(node =>

                  node.nodeType == 1 && node.matches("[personalized-message*='y']")

                );

                if(hasPersonalizaedMessage){

                  var push_token = {"mbox_name" : "ET_NotificationBar", "at_res" : {"product_list" : [],

					    "click_track_selector" : ["[personalized-message='y'] .c-notification-banner__link","[personalized-message='yes'] .c-notification-banner__link"]

				  }};

				  _satellite.track("push_at_token", push_token);

                  observer.disconnect();

                  break;

                }

              }

            }

          };

          var observer = new MutationObserver(observerCallback);

          var observerOptions = {

            childList : true,

            subtree : true

          };

          

          if(observe_target){

            observer.observe(observe_target, overserverOptions);

          } else {

            _satellite.logger.warn("Target Element (NotiBar) does not exist !!!");

          }

          // end of mutation observer

          

          if(token["experience.name"] == "CC_PDPPromtion"){

              checkElementInterval = setInterval(triggerAtNotiClickEvent, 100);

          }

          

        }

      });



  }); 

}



function checkAdobeTarget() {

  if (window.adobe && window.adobe.target) {

    clearInterval(checkAdobeTargetInterval); // interval을 멈춤

    setAdobeTargetEventHandler();

  }

}



checkAdobeTargetInterval = setInterval(checkAdobeTarget, 100);







function isEmpty(val) { 

  return (val === undefined || val == null || val.length <= 0) ? true : false; 

} 



function key(obj) { 

   return Object.keys(obj) 

  .map(function(k) { return k + "" + obj[k]; }) 

  .join(""); 

} 



function distinct(arr) { 

  var result = arr.reduce(function(acc, e) { 

    acc[key(e)] = e; 

    return acc; 

  }, {}); 



  return Object.keys(result) 

  .map(function(k) { return result[k]; }); 

} 

</script>

  <script>_satellite["_runScript2"](function(event, target, Promise) {

window.at_res_all_debug = [];



// GA Variable Set w/ AT Response Token

document.addEventListener(adobe.target.event.REQUEST_SUCCEEDED, function(e) {  

    var tokens = e.detail.responseTokens;

	var mbox_name = e.detail.mbox;

    var ecid = _satellite.getVisitorId().getMarketingCloudVisitorID();

    window.at_evt_all = e;

    window.at_res_all = e.detail;

    window.at_res_all_debug.push(window.at_res_all);

    window.at_res_tokens = tokens;

  

    if (isEmpty(tokens)) { 

      return; 

    } 

  

    var uniqueTokens = distinct(tokens); 

    uniqueTokens.forEach(function(token) {      

      

          // GA Impression Track

          // new

          //window.dataLayer.push({

          var at_token = {

            "event" : "at_impression",

            "at_marketingCloudId" : ecid,

            "at_categoryAffinity" : token["profile.categoryAffinity"],

            "at_activityName" : token["activity.name"],

            "at_experienceName" : token["experience.name"],

            "at_parameterName" : token["profile.at_parameter"]

            // click_track_selector ??

          }

          _satellite.track("push_at_token",{"mbox_name" : mbox_name, "at_token" : at_token});

          //})

          

          //for global-target-mbox

          if(mbox_name == (undefined || null)){

            mbox_name = "global-target-mbox";

            dataLayer.push(at_token)

          }

          



       // end of token process

      

    });

   

    _satellite.logger.warn("Target Response Token Returned !!!");

  

});

  return (val === undefined || val == null || val.length <= 0) ? true : false; 

}

   return Object.keys(obj) 

  .map(function(k) { return k + "" + obj[k]; }) 

  .join(""); 

} 



function distinct(arr) { 

  var result = arr.reduce(function(acc, e) { 

    acc[key(e)] = e; 

    return acc; 

  }, {}); 



  return Object.keys(result) 

  .map(function(k) { return result[k]; }); 

}

  <script>_satellite["_runScript3"](function(event, target, Promise) {

adobe.target.getOffer({   

    "mbox": "ET_PLP_PD0001",

    "params": {

        "mapped_category": _satellite.getVar("CC - user category")

    },

    "success": function(offer) {    

        console.log(offer)

        _satellite.at_offer = offer;

        var audience = _satellite.at_offer[0].content[0].audience; // example: var audience = "monitor"



        if(audience == "all visitors"){

            //for default content

            _satellite.track("push_at_token", {"mbox_name" : "ET_PLP_PD0001", "at_res" : {

                "click_track_selector" : ".PD0001 [data-banners]"

            }});

        }

        else{



         

            var at_offer_content = offer[0].content;

            var parser = new DOMParser();

            var parsedHTML = parser.parseFromString(at_offer_content, "text/html");

            var newBanner = parsedHTML.querySelector('[data-banners]').getAttribute('data-banners');

            _satellite.PD0001Content = JSON.parse(newBanner);

            var stringNewBanner = JSON.stringify(_satellite.PD0001Content)

          

            document.querySelector('.PD0001 [data-banners]').setAttribute('data-banners',stringNewBanner);

            // at response token push

            _satellite.track("push_at_token", {"mbox_name" : "ET_PLP_PD0001", "at_res" : {

            "click_track_selector" : ".PD0001 [data-banners]"

            }});

        }   

    },   

    "error": function(status, error) {           

        console.log('Error', status, error); 

    } 

});

                 <p>*Prices, promotions and availability may vary by store and online. Prices subject to change without notice. Quantities are limited. Check with your local retailers for final price and availability.</p>

              <div class="c-footer__text-wrap"> 

               <div class="c-footer__inner"> 

                <div class="c-footer__text--more folded" id="seoArea"> 

                 <p>OLED TV brings breath-taking clarity and detail to your living room. Stream 4K HDR content from Netflix, Sky or Prime Video.  Key benefits of LG OLED TVs:  </p> 

                 <p>• Pioneering pixels: Self-lighting pixels automatically switch on and off without the need for a backlight.  </p> 

                 <p>• Perfect black: With no light passing through the pixels, unprecedented levels of black can be realised.  </p> 

                 <p>• Zero blur: The fastest video games stay smooth, as OLED TVs reduce motion blur by processing frames more than 1,000 times faster than LED TVs.  </p> 

                 <p>• 4K resolution: OLED TVs are 4K too. Experience four times the detail of a Full HD TV and see Netflix, Prime Video and Sky* at their best.  </p> 

                 <p>• Netflix-approved: LG OLED achieved Netflix Recommended TV status in 2017 and 2018 for its fast and user-friendly experience.  </p> 

                 <p>• Dolby Vision™: LG OLED TVs are compatible with HDR formats including Dolby Vision, which enhances your picture frame by frame.  </p> 

                 <p>• Dolby Atmos® TVs: LG OLED TVs recreate the moving sound cinema experience of Dolby Atmos in your home.  </p> 

                 <p>• High frame rate: OLED TVs can run games and movies at 120 frames per second – the new high frame rate standard. Find out more about LG OLED TVs .  *Subscription packages required where appropriate</p> 

                </div> <button class="more" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="seoArea" data-text="More,Close">More</button> 

               </div> 

              </div>

    function onLoadCompleted({ response: { error }}) {

      //error can be true/false  

      if (error) {

        // Sprinklr chat could not be loaded

        console.log(error);

      } else {

        // Sprinklr chat is loaded

      if ((window.location.host.indexOf("lg.com") > -1) && (window.location.href.indexOf("/uk/orderconfirmed/") > -1)) {

          var orderNode = document.getElementsByClassName("cmp-text font-w-semibold-24 font-m-semibold-16")[0];

          var orderID;

          if (orderNode) {

            orderID = orderNode.textContent;

          }

 

         var productCount = 0;

         [...document.getElementsByClassName("c-checkout-ordered__product__text-box__desc-qty")].forEach((ele) => {

             if (ele) {

               productCount = productCount + Number(ele.textContent.split('Qty:  : ')[1]);

             }

         });

 

         var productPrice = document.getElementsByClassName("cmp-text font-w-semibold-32 font-m-semibold-20")[0].textContent;

          window.sprChat('updateConversationContext', {

            context: {

                "_c_6439634f9b7f66381458fc80": [orderID], //internalorderID

                "_c_6464e4e450fb210c8975a4ba": [productCount.toString()], // productCount

                "_c_6464eb7650fb210c897ca692": [productPrice], // productPrice

                "_c_643967139b7f6638145d06af": ['Yes'], //internalplaced

            },

            includeDeleted: true,

            filters: {

                    filterType: 'NIN',    

                }],

            }

          });

        }

      }

    }

    window.sprChat('subscribeToUpdate', {

      topic: 'loadCompleted',

      subscriber: onLoadCompleted,
